	(function() {
		/*
		|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
		| PRELOAD
		|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
		*/
		var preloadInit = function() {


				var preloadedScreen = Fizzmod.Utils.getCookie("preloaded-screen");

				if (preloadedScreen) {
					$("#preload-wrapper").hide();
				} else {
					Fizzmod.Utils.setCookie("preloaded-screen", 1, 1);
				}

				var callcenterStoreCookie = Fizzmod.Utils.getCookie("callcenter-store");
				if(callcenterStoreCookie) {
					// Set label in header
					$(document).ready(function() {
						$("#active-store-name-label").text(callcenterStoreCookie)
					});

					$("#preload-wrapper, #store-locality").hide();
				}

				if ($("#preload-wrapper").length != 0) preloadStart(); // If preload exist show animation


		}

		var preloadStart = function(start) {
			var PathLoader = function(el) {
				this.el = el;
				// clear stroke
				this.el.style.strokeDasharray = this.el.style.strokeDashoffset = this.el.getTotalLength();
			}
			PathLoader.prototype._draw = function(val) {
				this.el.style.strokeDashoffset = this.el.getTotalLength() * (1 - val);
			}
			PathLoader.prototype.setProgress = function(val) {
				this._draw(val);
			}
			PathLoader.prototype.setProgressFn = function(fn) {
				if (typeof fn === 'function') {
					fn(this);
				}
			}

			var progress = 0
			var simulationFn = function(instance) {
				var interval = setInterval(function() {
					progress = Math.min(progress + Math.random() * 0.1, 1);
					instance.setProgress(progress);

					// reached the end
					if (progress === 1) {
						clearInterval(interval);
						preloadEnd();
					}
				}, 100);
			};

			var loaderInnerCircle = $("#preload-loader-circle");
			var loader = new PathLoader(loaderInnerCircle[0]);

			$(document).on("animationend webkitAnimationEnd", "#preload-wrapper .loader", function(event) {
				if(event.originalEvent.animationName == "animInitialHeader") {
					start = false;
					loader.setProgressFn(simulationFn);
				}
				if(event.originalEvent.animationName == "animLoadedLoader") {
					setTimeout(function() {
						$("#preload-wrapper").hide();
					}, 200)
				}
			});

			if(start) {
				progress = 0;
				loader.setProgressFn(simulationFn);
			}
		}

		var preloadEnd = function() {
			var preloadWrapper = $("#preload-wrapper");
			preloadWrapper.removeClass("loading").addClass("loaded");
		}

		preloadInit();
	})();
</script><!-- Preload Screen --><!-- /GLOBAL TEMPLATES --><!-- Overlay Filters Mobile --><div id="filters-mobile" class="overlay" style="display: none;"><div class="overlay__wrapper"><button type="button" class="overlay__close"><div class="font-icn cross"></div></button><div class="overlay__content filters-mobile"><div class="filters-mobile__main-title"><span class="font-icn filter"></span><span class="text">FILTRAR</span></div><div class="filters-mobile__middle-content"><div class="filters-mobile__titles"></div><div class="filters-mobile__groups"></div></div><div class="filters-mobile__actions"><button class="filters-mobile__action filters-mobile__action--reset-filters btn gray-border"><span class="font-icn cross"></span><span class="text">ELIMINAR FILTROS</span></button><button class="filters-mobile__action filters-mobile__action--save-and-apply btn primary-border disabled"><span class="font-icn go-back"></span><span class="text">GUARDAR Y APLICAR MÁS FILTROS</span></button><button class="filters-mobile__action filters-mobile__action--apply btn second-border disabled">

function BdwLimitAddProducts(){
    if (vtexjs != undefined && vtexjs != null && vtexjs.checkout.orderForm.items.length > 0) {
        var data = vtexjs.checkout.orderForm.items;
        $.each(data,function (i,item) {
            var bdwbutton = $('button[data-productid="'+item.productId+'"]');
            if(bdwbutton.length === 0){
                return true;
            }
            var bdwlimit = bdwbutton.closest('.product-item__controls').find('.product-quantity__input').attr('onchange').match(/\d/g);

            if (bdwlimit != null && item.quantity >= parseInt(bdwlimit[0])) {
                bdwbutton.removeClass('product-item__add-to-cart');
                bdwbutton.attr('onclick', 'return false;');
            }
        })
    }
}

function BwdInputLimitCart(element, limit){
    try{
        if (limit == 0 || limit ==null) {
            limit=50;
        }
        limit = (limit == null) ? 0 : limit;
        var newvalue = $(element).val();
        if(limit != 0 && newvalue > limit){
            $(element).val(limit);
            $(element).blur();
        }
    }
    catch(e){
        console.log(e);
    }
}
function clearProductsBwnGond(IdCode,sufix) {    
    try {
        var dataAdic = " kg";
        if ($('#brandwProductGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().indexOf(',') > -1 || $('#brandwProductGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().indexOf('.') > -1)   dataAdic = " kg";
         else 
            dataAdic = "";
        
        var actual = parseFloat($('input[id=cantProdBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val().replace(' kg', ''));
        var peso = parseFloat($('#brandwProductGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().replace(' kg', ''));
        if ((actual - peso) <= 0) {
            $('input[id=cantProdBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val(peso + dataAdic);            
            $('#clearProductsBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).removeClass('brandwdecrease');
            $('#clearProductsBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).addClass('brandwdecreasedisable');
        } else {
            $('#clearProductsBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).removeClass('brandwdecreasedisable');
            $('#clearProductsBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).addClass('brandwdecrease');            
            if (dataAdic == "") {
                $('input[id=cantProdBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val((actual - peso));
            } else {
                var pesoFinal = (actual - peso).toFixed(2);
                if (pesoFinal[pesoFinal.length - 1] == '0')
                    pesoFinal = pesoFinal.substr(0, pesoFinal.length - 1);

                $('input[id=cantProdBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val(pesoFinal + dataAdic);
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {}
}
function addProductsBwnGond(IdCode, sufix, limit) {
    try {  
        if(limit == null) limit = 0;  
        var dataAdic = " kg";
        if ($('#brandwProductGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().indexOf(',') > -1 || $('#brandwProductGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().indexOf('.') > -1)
            dataAdic = " kg";  else dataAdic = "";      
        var actual = parseFloat($('input[id=cantProdBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val().replace(' kg', ''));

        if (limit === 0) {
           limit = 50;
        }

        if (limit != 0 && actual >= limit) {
           return;
        }
        var peso = parseFloat($('#brandwProductGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode ).val().replace(' kg', ''));
        $('button#addProductsBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).removeClass('brandwdecreasedisable');
        $('button#clearProductsBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).addClass('brandwdecrease');
        if (dataAdic == "") 
            $('input[id=cantProdBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val((actual + peso));
        else {
            var pesoFinal = (actual + peso).toFixed(2);
            if (pesoFinal[pesoFinal.length - 1] == '0')
                pesoFinal = pesoFinal.substr(0, pesoFinal.length - 1);

            $('input[id=cantProdBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val(pesoFinal + dataAdic);
        }
    } catch (e) {}
}
function AddToMiniCartBraindGond(url, IdCode, sufix) {    
    try {
        var quantity = Math.round(parseFloat($('input[id=cantProdBwnGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val()) / parseFloat($('#brandwProductGond-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val()));
        url = url + "&redirect=false";
        url = url.replace('qty=1', 'qty=' + quantity)
        $.ajax({
            url: url,
            dataType: 'json',
            cache: false,
            async: true,
            timeout: 9000,
            data: '',
            success: function(data) {
                vtexjs.checkout.getOrderForm()
                if($("#minicart-navigation").length>0){
                    $("#minicart-navigation").css('display', 'block');
                }
                else{
                    if (document.URL.toLowerCase().indexOf('cart')>-1){
                        $('.span.font-icn.shopping-cart').css('display','none');
                        $('.bdw-loader').css({
                               "display":"block",
                               "width": "30px",
                               "height": "30px",
                               "margin":"auto",
                               "top":"0",
                               "right":"0",
                               "left":"0",
                               "background":"0 0",
                               "position": "absolute",
                            })
                        setTimeout(function() {
                            $('.bdw-product-add-to-cart').css('display','inline');
                            $('.span.font-icn.shopping-cart').css('display','inline');
                            $('.bdw-loader').css('display','none');

                        }, 500);
                    }
                }
                BdwLimitAddProducts();
            },
            error: function(xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {}
        });
    } catch (e) {}
}

function bdwSetLinksCollection(urlcheck)
{
    var bdwCollectionCategory = braindwlGetCategoryCyber();
    if (urlcheck.indexOf('/buscapagina?sl') != -1 && bdwCollectionCategory!='' )
    {
        console.log('enter');

        var bdwObGrid = $('.product-item a.product-item__image-link[href$="/p"]').not("[href*='/p?CatCyber=']");
        $.each( bdwObGrid, function( i, val ) {
            bdwObGrid[i].href = bdwObGrid[i].href +'?CatCyber='+bdwCollectionCategory; 
        });

        bdwObGrid = $('.product-item a.product-item__name[href$="/p"]').not("[href*='/p?CatCyber=']");
        $.each( bdwObGrid, function( i, val ) {
            bdwObGrid[i].href =bdwObGrid[i].href +'?CatCyber='+bdwCollectionCategory; 
        });

        bdwObGrid = $('div.product-item.gotten-product-item-data[data-uri$="/p"]').not("[data-uri*='/p?CatCyber=']");
        $.each( bdwObGrid, function( i, val ) {console.log($(bdwObGrid[i]).attr('data-uri'));
            $(bdwObGrid[i]).attr('data-uri', $(bdwObGrid[i]).attr('data-uri') +'?CatCyber='+bdwCollectionCategory); 
        });   
    }
}

{

    if ( bdwCa[bnwi].indexOf("VTEXSC") > -1) {
     
return bdwCa[bnwi].split('=')[2];
    }
}
}catch(e){console.log(e);}
return '';
}
function GetFoundWords() {
    var t = "",
        e = /(<([^>]+)>)/gi,
        n = document.body.innerText;
    n = n.replace(e, " ").toLowerCase();
    var r = "{wordstofind}".split(",");
    for (i = 0; i < r.length; i++) -1 != n.indexOf(r[i]) && (t += r[i] + ",");
    return t
}

function formatstringBnw(s) {
var r=s.toLowerCase();
            r = r.replace(new RegExp(/\s/g),"");
            r = r.replace(new RegExp(/[àáâãäå]/g),"a");
            r = r.replace(new RegExp(/[èéêë]/g),"e");
            r = r.replace(new RegExp(/[ìíîï]/g),"i");
            r = r.replace(new RegExp(/ñ/g),"n");                
            r = r.replace(new RegExp(/[òóôõö]/g),"o");
            r = r.replace(new RegExp(/[ùúûü]/g),"u");
            
 return r;
}
function braindNdwGetProperty(t) {
    // VTEX
    try {
        if (typeof skuJson_0 != "undefined") {
            if (typeof skuJson_0.skus != "undefined") {
                if (skuJson_0.skus.length > 0) {
                    var braindwVtx_script = $('script:contains("vtex.events.addData")').html();
                    var catName = formatstringBnw($('.bread-crumb ul li:nth-child(3) a')[0].text);
                    var braindwVtx_json_ld = braindwVtx_script.substring(braindwVtx_script.indexOf('{'), braindwVtx_script.lastIndexOf('}') + 1);
                    if (braindwVtx_json_ld.length) {
                        var braindwVtx_json_pars = JSON.parse(braindwVtx_json_ld);
                        if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:title') {
                            return skuJson_0.skus[0].skuname;
                        }
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:image') {
                            return skuJson_0.skus[0].image;
                        }
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:url') {
                            return $('link[rel=canonical]').attr('href');
                        }
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:category') {
                            return braindwVtx_json_pars.productCategoryName;
                        }
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:categorycode') {
                            return braindwVtx_json_pars.productCategoryId;
                        }
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:categorypname') {
                            return braindwVtx_json_pars.productDepartmentName;
                        }
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:categorypcode') {                           
                            try{                                
                                return braindwVtx_json_pars.productDepartmentId + catName;
                            }catch(e){}
                            return braindwVtx_json_pars.productDepartmentId;
                        }
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:brand') {
                            return braindwVtx_json_pars.productBrandName;
                        }
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:codeproduct') {
                            return braindwVtx_json_pars.productId;
                        }       
                        else if (t.toLowerCase() == 'og:price') {
                            if(skuJson_0.skus[0].bestPriceFormated.indexOf('S/.') >-1 ){
                                return skuJson_0.skus[0].bestPriceFormated.replace('S/. ','');
                            }else{
                                return skuJson_0.skus[0].bestPriceFormated.replace('S/ ','');
                            }
                            
                        }                               
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    } catch (ex) { }

    return "";
}

function BraindwLoadEvent(){
$(document).on("click", "._braindwTriggerClick", function(event){    
    var bdwAttrCat = 'banner';
    var bdwAttrEti = 'default';
    var bdwAttrSku= '';   
    try{bdwAttrCat=$(this).attr('bw-section');}
    catch(err){}
    try{bdwAttrEti=$(this).attr('bw-title');}
    catch(err){}
    try{bdwAttrSku=$(this).attr('bw-sku');}
    catch(err){}
    BraindwPushEvent(bdwAttrCat,bdwAttrEti,bdwAttrSku);
});
    BdwLimitAddProducts();
}

function BraindwPushEvent(cat,eti,sku)
{
    try {
        if(sku!='') eti = eti+'['+sku+']';
        ga('send','event','ga-braindw',cat,eti);
    }
    catch(err) {}
}

function GetBraindSearchMade(){
try {
    var bnwsc = '';
    ca = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).split(';');
    for (var bnwi = 0; bnwi < ca.length; bnwi++) {
        if (ca[bnwi].indexOf("VTEXSC") > -1) {
            bnwsc = ca[bnwi].split('=')[2];
            if (bnwsc.indexOf('&')>-1)
                bnwsc = bnwsc.split('&')[0];
        }
    }
    if (bnwsc=='') bnwsc=3;
    var braindwDataJSON = {
        dataset: JSON.stringify(dataLayer),
        page: '', 
        url: window.location.toString(),
        urlb: "https://s.braindw.com/Script/braindw/wong_peru_produccion_fsrff?hs=Sat Apr 21 2018 10:00:38 GMT-0300 (Hora estándar de Argentina)",
        HashIdSession: '',
        branchOffice: bnwsc
    };
    $.ajax({
        url: "https://p.braindw.com/Api/Data/Capture",
        type: "post",
        timeout: 25000,
        data: JSON.stringify(braindwDataJSON),
        contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
        success: function (data) { },
        error: function () { },
        xhrFields: {
            withCredentials: true
        },
        crossDomain: true
    });
} catch (err) {restaurarBotones();}
}
function IsSearchMadeUser() {
    $.ajax({
        url: 'https://u.braindw.com/api/VtexApi/IsSearchMade/',
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        async: true,
        xhrFields: {
            withCredentials: true
        },
        crossDomain: true,
        timeout: 12000,
        data: 'token=<%TOKEN%>&company=wongfood&url=' + window.location.host + '&BWGuid=',
        success: function (data) {
            if (data ==true)
                ShowSearch();
        },
        error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) { }
    });
}

function ShowProduct(position, totalProduct) {
    $(".tab-pane.ndwdropditems").css('display', 'none');
    $(".bdwsearchitem" + position).css('display', 'block'); 
    for (var bwdi=0; bwdi<totalProduct;bwdi++)
    {
        $(".bwduser"+ bwdi).css('background-color',''); 
    }
    $(".bwduser"+ position).css('background-color','antiquewhite'); 
}
function GetSearchMadeUser()
{
    var bnwsc = '';
    ca = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).split(';');
    for (var bnwi = 0; bnwi < ca.length; bnwi++) {
        if (ca[bnwi].indexOf("VTEXSC") > -1) {
            bnwsc = ca[bnwi].split('=')[2];
        }
    }
    if (bnwsc=='') bnwsc=3;// testing 
    $.ajax({
        url: 'https://u.braindw.com/api/VtexApi/GetSearchMade/',
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        async: true,
        xhrFields: {
            withCredentials: true
        },
        crossDomain: true,
        timeout: 20000,
        data: 'token=<%TOKEN%>&company=wongfood&url=' + window.location.host + '&BWGuid=&branchOffice=' + bnwsc,
        success: function (data) {
            BraindwRendeSearch(data);
        },
        error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) { restaurarBotones(); }
    });     
}

function restaurarBotones()
{
    $("#bwnSearch").html('<button class="braindw_ultbwm2" id="bwnSearch" onclick="CargarBusquedas();"><span class="font-icn braindw_search_list"></span><span class="text" id="bwnSearch" style="letter-spacing:.35px;font-size:.78rem"">MIS ÚLTIMAS <br>BUSQUEDAS</span></button>');
    
    $("#BrwSearchMovil").html('<div class="search-mobile__tab active" data-content="multiple-search" onclick="GetSearchMadeUser();" style="width: 100%;border-bottom: none;"><span class="font-icn search"></span><span class="text" style="color: #000">MIS ÚLTIMAS <br>BÚSQUEDAS</span></div>');
}
function BraindwViewProducts() {
    $('.box').hide();
    $('#' + $('#braindw-ultmob2').val()).show();
    $(".btndelbox").click(function () {
        $(".box").hide();
        $("#braindw-ultmob2").val('0')
        $("#braindwMySearch2").hide();
    });
    
    $('.braindw-btndel').click(function () {
        $(".box").hide();
        $("#braindw-ultmob2").val('0')
        $("#braindwMySearch2").hide();
    });
}
function DeleteSearch() {
    $.ajax({
        url: 'https://p.braindw.com/Api/Data/ClearMasterDataSearh/',
        dataType: 'json',
        cache: false,
        async: true,
        type: 'GET',
        xhrFields: {
            withCredentials: true
        },
        crossDomain: true,
        timeout:12000,
        data: 'company=wongfood',
        success: function (data) {
            $(".box").hide();
            $('.dropdown-menu').remove();
            $('.tab-pane,.ndwdropditems').css('display', 'none');
            $('.ndwmaindrop').css({
                "width": "234px",
                "height": "76px",
            });
            Borrarcaja();
            try {
                $(".braindw_search").css('display', 'none');
                $(".ndwmaindrop").css('display', 'none');
            } catch (e) {}
        },
        error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) { restaurarBotones(); }
    });
}
function Borrarcaja() {
    $('.ndwmaindrop').hide();
    $('.braindw-ultmoberr2').hide();
    $(".box").hide();
    $("#braindw-ultmob2").val('0')
    $("#braindwMySearch2").hide();
}
function Mostrar() {
    if ($(".ndwdropdmenu,.ndwmaindrop").css('display') == 'block') {
        $(".ndwdropdmenu,.ndwmaindrop").css('display', 'none');
        $(".tab-content").css('display', 'none');
    }
    else {
        $(".ndwdropdmenu,.ndwmaindrop").show();
        $(".tab-content").show();
    }
}

function MostrarMovil()
{
    $('#braindwMySearch2').css('display', 'block');
}
function Delbusq() {
    $(".braindw-delbusq").click(function () {
        $('.msgdelbusq').css('display', 'none');
        $('.tab-pane,.ndwdropditems').css('display', 'none');
        $('.braindw-ultmoberr2').show();
    });
    DeleteSearch();
}

function validateEmail(email) {
    var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
    return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
}

$(document).ready( function() {
    GetBraindSearchMade();
    IsSearchMadeUser();
    $(document).on('click','#btn-client-pre-email,#newsletterButtonOK', function (element) {
        var email = $('#client-pre-email,#newsletterClientEmail').val();
        if (validateEmail(email)) {
            try {
                fetch('https://s.braindw.com/tracking/SetCookiesNdway?email=' + email + '&company=wong_peru_produccion', {
                    credentials: "include",
                    mode: 'no-cors',
                    method: 'POST',
                })
                .then(function(resp) {
                    return resp.text();
                })
                .then(function(data) {
                    braindw_pushInfo(email);
                    return false;
                })
                .catch(function(ex) {
                    console.log(ex);
                });
            } catch (e) { }
        }
    });
}); 

function parseJwt (token) {
    try{
    var base64Url = token.split('.')[1];
    var base64 = base64Url.replace('-', '+').replace('_', '/');
    return JSON.parse(window.atob(base64));
    }catch(e)
    { return null;}
}

if ($('.user-menu__user-name').length>0 )
{
    try{
        var cookie_user = Cookies.get('VtexIdclientAutCookie_wongfood');
        var token = parseJwt(cookie_user);
        $.ajax({
            url: "https://s.braindw.com/tracking/SetCookiesNdway",
            type: 'POST',
            xhrFields: {
                withCredentials: true
            },
            dataType: 'jsonp',
            data: 'email='+ token.sub + '&company=wong_peru_produccion ',
            success: function(data) {
                return false;       
            }
        });
    }catch(e)
    {}
}
try {
    $(document).ajaxSuccess(function (e, r, a) {
        try {
             if (a.url.length >= 36) {
                if (a.url.toLowerCase().substring(0, 36).toLowerCase() == '/wongfood/dataentities/re/documents/') {

                    var bdwCode = a.url.split('/')[a.url.split('/').length - 1].split('?')[0];
                    var bdwView = $("[data-id='" + bdwCode + "']").first();
                    if (bdwView.length > 0) {
                        var bdwViewTitle = bdwView.find(".product-item__name").first().attr("title");
                        var bdwViewImageLink = bdwView.find(".product-item__image-link").first().attr("href");
                        var bdwViewImageSrc = bdwView.find(".product-item__image-link img").first().attr('src');
                        var bdwViewPrice = bdwView.find('.product-prices__value--best-price').text();
                        console.log('$(document).ajaxSuccess>' + bdwViewPrice);
                        if (bdwCode.length > 0 && bdwViewTitle.length > 0 && bdwViewImageLink.length > 0 && bdwViewImageSrc.length > 0) {

                            BraindwPushView(bdwCode, encodeURIComponent(bdwViewTitle), encodeURIComponent(bdwViewImageLink), encodeURIComponent(bdwViewImageSrc), 0, bdwViewPrice);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

        } catch (c) { console.log(c); }

    })
} catch (err) { console.log(err); }

function BraindwPushView(code, title, link, image,iscart,price) {
    try {
        var _braindwTimeoutService = 5000;
        var bndwsc = '';
        var bdwca = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).split(';');
        for (var bnwi = 0; bnwi < bdwca.length; bnwi++) {
            if (bdwca[bnwi].indexOf("VTEXSC") > -1) {
                bndwsc = bdwca[bnwi].split('=')[2];
                if (bndwsc.indexOf('&') > -1)
                    bndwsc = bnwsc.split('&')[0];
            }
        }
        var o = document.createElement("script");
        BraindwGetCapture(code, title, link, image, iscart, price);
        var i = document.createElement("script");
        i.async = !0, i.src = 'https://s.braindw.com/tracking/track?HASH=wong_peru_produccion_fsrff&branchOffice=' + bndwsc + '&wordsfound=&buyer=&name=&lastname=&gender=&country=&state=&city=&email=&u=' + link, i.charset = "UTF-8", document.head.appendChild(i);
    } catch (c) { console.log(c); }
}
function braindw_pushInfo(email) {
    try {
        let _bwDataset = {};

        let _currentSessionDate = braindw_getSessionDate();
        if (_currentSessionDate) {
            _bwDataset.sessionDate = _currentSessionDate;
        }       
        // get product
        let _currentProduct = braindw_getProduct();
        if (_currentProduct) {
            _bwDataset.product = _currentProduct;
        }
        // get category 
        let _currentCategory = braindw_getCategory();
        if (_currentCategory) {
            _bwDataset.category = _currentCategory;
        }       
        // get cart 
        let _currentCartOpened = braindw_getCatOpened();
        if (_currentCartOpened) {
            _bwDataset.cartOpened = _currentCartOpened;
        }else{
            _currentCartOpened = braindw_getCatClosed();
            if (_currentCartOpened) 
                _bwDataset.cartClosed = _currentCartOpened;
        }
        // ESTO VER como hacer en vtex. NO SE SI hace falta porque te cookeas cuando te logeas
        let _emailGuest = '';
        if (email === '' || email === undefined) {
            try{
                _emailGuest= $('.email').text();
            }
            catch(e){}
            try{
                if (_emailGuest=='') _emailGuest = $('.cconf-client-email').text();
            }catch(e){}
            try {
                if (Json_user != null) {
                    if (Json_user.SetUser != null) {
                        if (Json_user.SetUser.UserEmail != null && Json_user.SetUser.UserEmail != '') {
                            _emailGuest = Json_user.SetUser.UserEmail;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }catch (e) { }
        }else{
            _emailGuest = email;
        }

        let braindwDataJSON = {
            emailguest: _emailGuest,
            dataset: encodeURI(JSON.stringify(_bwDataset)),
            page: '',//,document.documentElement.innerHTML,
            url: window.location.href.split('?')[0],
            urlb: "https://s.braindw.com/Script/braindw/wong_peru_produccion_fsrff?",
            BranchOffice:  GetSC_Braindw()
        };

        $.ajax({
            url: "https://p.braindw.com/Api/Data/Capture",
            type: "post",
            timeout: 9000,
            data: JSON.stringify(braindwDataJSON),
            contentType: 'application/json; charset=utf-8',
            success: function (data) { },
            error: function () { },
            xhrFields: {
                withCredentials: true
            },
            crossDomain: true
        });
    }
    catch (err) {
        console.log('Error------------>', err);
    }
}
function braindw_getSessionDate() {
    let result = null;
     try {
        let SalesChannel = GetSC_Braindw();
        result = {
            SalesChannel: SalesChannel,
        };
    } catch (e) {
        console.log('braindw_getSessionDate error ', e);
    }
    return result;
}
function braindw_getProduct() {
    let result = null;
    if (document.URL.indexOf('/p')==-1) return null;
    try {
        let ProductCode = "";
        let Title = "";
        let PriceOnline = "";
        let Brand = "";
        let Category = "";
        let CategoryCode = "";
        let UrlImage = "";
        let UrlProduct = window.location.href;
        if (UrlProduct.indexOf('?')>-1)
        {
            UrlProduct = UrlProduct.split('?')[0];
        }
        if (typeof skuJson_0 != "undefined") {
            if (typeof skuJson_0.skus != "undefined") {
                if (skuJson_0.skus.length > 0) {
                    Title = skuJson_0.skus[0].skuname;
                    UrlImage = skuJson_0.skus[0].image;
                    PriceOnline = skuJson_0.skus[0].bestPriceFormated;
                    PriceOnline = PriceOnline.replace("$","").replace("S/.", "").replace("S/", "").trim();
                }
            }
        }         
        var braindwVtx_script = $('script:contains("vtex.events.addData")').html();
        var braindwVtx_json_ld = braindwVtx_script.substring(braindwVtx_script.indexOf('{'), braindwVtx_script.lastIndexOf('}') + 1);
        if (braindwVtx_json_ld.length) {
            var braindwVtx_json_pars = JSON.parse(braindwVtx_json_ld);
            ProductCode =  braindwVtx_json_pars.productId;
            Brand = braindwVtx_json_pars.productBrandName;
            Category = braindwVtx_json_pars.productCategoryName;            
            CategoryCode = braindwVtx_json_pars.productCategoryId;          
        }
        if (ProductCode && Title && PriceOnline && Brand &&
            Category && CategoryCode && UrlImage && UrlProduct) {
            result = {
                ProductCode: ProductCode,
                Title: Title,
                PriceOnline: PriceOnline,
                Brand: Brand,
                Category: Category,
                CategoryCode: CategoryCode,
                UrlImage: UrlImage,
                UrlProduct: UrlProduct,
                BranchOffice:  GetSC_Braindw()
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.log('braindw_getProduct error ', e);
    }
    return result;
}
function GetSC_Braindw(){
    var bnwsc = '';
    ca = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie).split(';');
    for (var bnwi = 0; bnwi < ca.length; bnwi++) {
        if (ca[bnwi].indexOf("VTEXSC") > -1) {
            try{
                bnwsc = ca[bnwi].split('=')[2];
                if (bnwsc=='')
                    bnwsc = ca[bnwi].split('=')[1];
            }catch(e){
                bnwsc = ca[bnwi].split('=')[1];
            }
        }
    }
    return bnwsc;   
}
function braindw_getCategory() {
    let result = null;
    var braindw_url = document.URL;
    if (braindw_url.indexOf('/p')>-1 && braindw_url.indexOf('/cart')>-1) return result;
    try {
        let Title = "";
        let CategoryCode = "";
        if (vtxctx.categoryId!=undefined) {
            CategoryCode = vtxctx.categoryId;
            Title = vtxctx.categoryName; 
        }
        if (Title && CategoryCode) {
            result = {
                Title: Title,
                CategoryCode: CategoryCode
            };
        }
    } catch (e) {
        //console.log('braindw_getCategory error ', e);
    }
    return result;
}

function braindw_getCatOpened() {    
    let result = null;
    var braindw_url = document.URL;
    //if (braindw_url.indexOf('/cart')==-1) return result;
    try {
        let CartNumber = "";
        let Items = [];
        
        let productRows = document.getElementsByClassName('product-item');
        if (productRows && productRows.length > 0) {
            for (let i = 0; i < productRows.length; i++) {              
                if ($(productRows[i]).prop('nodeName')=='DIV')
                    Items.push(Brainwd_addCartItemDiv(productRows[i]));
                else if ($(productRows[i]).prop('nodeName')=='TR')
                    Items.push(Brainwd_addCartItemTr(productRows[i]));            
            }
        } 
        result = {
            CartNumber: CartNumber,
            BranchOffice: GetSC_Braindw(),
            Items: Items
        }
    } catch (e) {
        //console.log('braindw_getCatOpened', e);
    }
    return result;
}

function Brainwd_addCartItemTr(braindw_lineCart)
{
    var imgUrl = $(braindw_lineCart).find('img').attr('src');
    var productCode =  $(braindw_lineCart).data('sku')
    var inpQuantity = $(braindw_lineCart).find('#item-quantity-' + productCode).val()
    var productTitle =  $($(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-name a')[0]).text().trim();                
    var productPriceTotal =$($(braindw_lineCart).find('.total-selling-price')).text().trim().replace(/[^\d.,-]/g, '');
    var pric =  '';
    pric = $(braindw_lineCart).find('.new-product-price').text().trim().replace(/[^\d.,-]/g, '');

    // falidar las comas 
    var cartItem = {
    ProductTitle :productTitle.trim(),
    ProductCode : productCode,
    ProductUrlImage : imgUrl,
    ProductQuantity :inpQuantity,
    ProductQuantityDetails : '',
    ProductPrice : pric,
    PriceTotal : productPriceTotal,
    Event :'Load'}

    return cartItem;    
}

function Brainwd_addCartItemDiv(braindw_lineCart)
{   
    var imgUrl = $(braindw_lineCart).find('a.product-item__image-wrapper').find('img').attr('src');
    var inpQuantity = $(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-item__cart-quantity').text().trim().replace('x','');
    var productTitle =  $(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-item__info').text().trim();              
    var productCode =  $(braindw_lineCart).data('id');
    var productPriceTotal = $($(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-item__subtotal')[0]).text().trim().replace(/[^\d.,-]/g, '');
    var productQuantityDetails =  $(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-quantity__input').val();
    // Payment
    var payments = '';
    var pric =  '';
    var pricText = '';
    var bdw_i_pre =0
    if($(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-prices__value').length>1)
        bdw_i_pre = 1;
    
    try{pric = $($(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-prices__value')[bdw_i_pre]).data('price').toString();
    }catch(e){
        try{pric = $($(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-prices__value')[bdw_i_pre+1]).data('price').toString();}catch(e){}
    }
    if ((pric==undefined && bdw_i_pre==1) || pric=='')
    {
        pric = $($(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-prices__value')[0]).data('price').toString();
    }   
    // validacion por si no tiene las comas o puntos.
    pricText = $($(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-prices__value')[bdw_i_pre]).html();
    if (pricText.indexOf('(')==-1 && pricText.toLowerCase().indexOf('kg')==-1)
    {
        pricText = $($(braindw_lineCart).find('.product-prices__value')[bdw_i_pre]).html().replace(/[^\d.,-]/g, '');
        if (pricText.indexOf('-')>-1)
        {
            pricText = pricText.split('-')[0];
        }
        if (pric!=undefined && pricText!=pric.toString())
        {
            pric = pricText;
        }   
    }
    var cartItem = {
    ProductTitle :productTitle.trim(),
    ProductCode : productCode,
    ProductUrlImage : imgUrl,
    ProductQuantity :inpQuantity,
    ProductQuantityDetails : productQuantityDetails,
    ProductPrice : pric,
    PriceTotal : productPriceTotal,
    Event :'Load'}
    return cartItem;    
}

function braindw_getCatClosed() {
    let result = null;
    var braindw_url = document.URL;
    if (braindw_url.toLowerCase().indexOf('/checkout/orderconfirmation') == -1 && 
        braindw_url.toLowerCase().indexOf('/checkout/orderplaced')==-1) return result;
    try {       
        let CartNumber = braindw_url.split('og=')[1];
        let Items = [];
        let productRows = document.getElementsByClassName('cconf-product bt b--light-gray');        
        if (productRows && productRows.length > 0) {
            for (let i = 0; i < productRows.length; i++) {
                Items.push(Brainwd_addCartItemTrClosed(productRows[i]));       
            }
        } 
        else
        {
            productRows = document.getElementsByClassName('orderform-product-table__row orderform-product-table__row--body');   
            if (productRows && productRows.length > 0) {
                for (let i = 0; i < productRows.length; i++) {
                    Items.push(Brainwd_addCartItemDivClosed(productRows[i])); 
                }
            } 
        }
        result = {
            CartNumber: CartNumber,
            Items: Items
        };
        
    } catch (e) {
        console.log('braindw_getCatClosed', e);
    }
    return result;
}

var _bdwTemporal;
function BraindwBindingAddToCartInitial(ob)
{
    var addItem = 1;
    _bdwTemporal = ob;
    //capture bannercategoria
    var parent = $(ob).closest('.braindw_bigbannercategorias');
    if (parent.length!=0)
    {
        var productId = $(ob).data('productid');
        var productTitle = parent.find('.braindw_bigbannercategoria_title a').text();
        var link = parent.find('.braindw_bigbannercategoria_title a').attr('href');
        var image = parent.find('a._braindwTriggerClick img').attr('src');
        var price = parent.find('li .braindw_bigbannercategoria_prices').text();
        BraindwPushView(productId, productTitle, link, image, 1, price);
    }else{
        // Capture.
    var parent = $(ob).closest('.gotten-product-item-data');
    var productId = $(ob).data('productid');
    var productTitle = parent.find('.product-item__info a').text();
    var link = parent.find('.product-item__info a').attr('href');
    var image = parent.find('.product-item__image-wrapper img').attr('src');
    var price = parent.find('.product-prices__value--best-price').text();    
    if (price != null && price != '')
    {
        price = price.replace('S/', '');
    }

    if (price == '' || price == null)
    {
        price = parent.find('.prateleira__best-price').text()
        if (price != null && price != '') {
            price = price.replace('S/', '');
        }
    }

    if (parent == null || parent.length==0)
    {
        console.log('parentnull');
        addItem = 0;
        try {

            if ($(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.prateleira__name').length != 0) {
                productId = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.prateleira__name').attr('bw-sku');
                productTitle = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.prateleira__name').text();
                price = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.prateleira__best-price').text().split('/')[1].split(' ')[0];
                image = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.prateleira__image img').attr('src');
                if (image === undefined) {
                    image = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement).find('.prateleira__image img').attr('src');
                }
                
                link = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.prateleira__name').attr('href');
            }
            else {

                image = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('img.braindw_indlateral2img').attr('src');

                if (image != null) {
                    productId = $($(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('a._braindwTriggerClick')[3]).attr('bw-sku');
                    productTitle = $($(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.braindw_indlateral2_title._braindwTriggerClick')).text();
                    price = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.braindw_best_price2').text().split('/')[1].split(' ')[0];
                    image = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('img.braindw_indlateral2img').attr('src');
                    link = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.braindw_indlateral2_title._braindwTriggerClick').attr('href');
                }
                else {
                        link = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.braindw_indlateral4_title._braindwTriggerClick').attr('href');
                        image = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('img.braindw_indlateral4img').attr('src');
                        productId = $($(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.product-add-to-cart.btn.add-to-cart.braindw_addToCart')).attr('data-productid');
                        productTitle = $($(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.braindw_indlateral4_title._braindwTriggerClick')).text();
                        price = $(_bdwTemporal.parentElement.parentElement).find('.braindw_best_price2').text().split('/')[1].split(' ')[0];
                }
            }
            if (link.indexOf('http') != -1 && image.indexOf('http') != -1 && price != null && price.length > 0) addItem = 1; 

        }
        catch(e){ console.log('return push'); return; }
    }

    if (addItem==1) BraindwPushView(productId, productTitle, link, image, 1, price);

    }
}

function CaptureCartFicha(){
     try {
      var tt = encodeURIComponent(braindNdwGetProperty("og:title")),
            i = escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:image")),
            s = escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:url")),
            c = escape(formatstringBnw(braindNdwGetProperty("og:category")));
            cc = escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:categorycode"));
            bd = escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:brand"));

        po = parseFloat(escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:price")).split('.')[0])
        ps = escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:pricesale"));
        pm = escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:promotion"));
        pol = '';
        if (ps != '' && ps.length > 1 && po != '') {
            pol = po;
            po = ps;
        }
        else
        {
            pol = '';
            ps = '';
        }           
        listcategories='';
        braindw_cpcode = escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:categorypcode"));
        
        if (document.URL.indexOf('CatCyber=cymom') > -1) {
            listcategories = document.URL.substring(document.URL.indexOf('CatCyber')).split('=')[1];
            braindw_cpcode= "cymom_3642";
        }else if (document.URL.indexOf('CatCyber') > -1) {
            listcategories = document.URL.substring(document.URL.indexOf('CatCyber')).split('=')[1];
            braindw_cpcode= "CartBT";
        }
        
        braindw_cpname =  escape(formatstringBnw(braindNdwGetProperty("og:categorypname")));            
        codprod = escape(braindNdwGetProperty("og:codeproduct"));
      
        var o = document.createElement("script");
        BraindwGetCapture(codprod, tt, s, i, 1, po);
         } catch (c) { console.log(c); }
}

function hideUltimasBusquedas()
{
    $('.minicart__action--toggle-open').click(function(event){
        $('.ndwmaindrop').hide();
    });
    $('#bwnSearch').click(function(event){
        $('.minicart--navigation').hide();
    });
}

function clearProductsBwnGondTopTen(IdCode,sufix) {    
    try {
        var dataAdic = " kg";
        if ($('#brandwProductGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().indexOf(',') > -1 || $('#brandwProductGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().indexOf('.') > -1) {
            dataAdic = " kg";
        } else {
            dataAdic = "";
        }

        var actual = parseFloat($('input[id=cantProdBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val().replace(' kg', ''));
        var peso = parseFloat($('#brandwProductGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().replace(' kg', ''));
        if ((actual - peso) <= 0) {
            $('input[id=cantProdBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val(peso + dataAdic);            
            $('#clearProductsBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).removeClass('brandwdecrease');
            $('#clearProductsBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).addClass('brandwdecreasedisable');
        } else {
            $('#clearProductsBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).removeClass('brandwdecreasedisable');
            $('#clearProductsBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).addClass('brandwdecrease');            
            if (dataAdic == "") {
                $('input[id=cantProdBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val((actual - peso));
            } else {
                var pesoFinal = (actual - peso).toFixed(2);
                if (pesoFinal[pesoFinal.length - 1] == '0')
                    pesoFinal = pesoFinal.substr(0, pesoFinal.length - 1);

                $('input[id=cantProdBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val(pesoFinal + dataAdic);
            }
        }
    } catch (e) {}
}

function addProductsBwnGondTopTen(IdCode, sufix, limit) {
    try {  
        if(limit == null) limit = 0;  
        var dataAdic = " kg";
        if ($('#brandwProductGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().indexOf(',') > -1 || $('#brandwProductGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val().indexOf('.') > -1)
            dataAdic = " kg";  else dataAdic = "";      
        var actual = parseFloat($('input[id=cantProdBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val().replace(' kg', ''));
        if (limit != 0 && actual == limit) {
           return;
        }

        var peso = parseFloat($('#brandwProductGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode ).val().replace(' kg', ''));        
        $('#clearProductsBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).removeClass('brandwdecreasedisable');
        $('#clearProductsBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).addClass('brandwdecrease');
        if (dataAdic == "") 
            $('input[id=cantProdBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val((actual + peso));
        else {
            var pesoFinal = (actual + peso).toFixed(2);
            if (pesoFinal[pesoFinal.length - 1] == '0')
                pesoFinal = pesoFinal.substr(0, pesoFinal.length - 1);

            $('input[id=cantProdBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val(pesoFinal + dataAdic);
        }
    } catch (e) {}
}
function AddToMiniCartBraindGondTopTen(url, IdCode, sufix) {    
    try {
        var quantity = Math.round(parseFloat($('input[id=cantProdBwnGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode +']').val()) / parseFloat($('#brandwProductGondTopTen-' + sufix + '-' + IdCode).val()));
        url = url + "&redirect=false";
        url = url.replace('qty=1', 'qty=' + quantity)
        $.ajax({
            url: url,
            dataType: 'json',
            cache: false,
            async: true,
            timeout: 9000,
            data: '',
            success: function(data) {
                vtexjs.checkout.getOrderForm()
                $("#minicart-navigation").css('display', 'block');
                BdwLimitAddProducts();
            },
            error: function(xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {}
        });
    } catch (e) {}
}

var bdw_arbol_category = '';
function Bdw_GetArbolCategoriesBySku() {
    try{
        var url = 'https://' + document.URL.split('/')[2] + '/api/catalog_system/pub/products/search';  
        var bdw_sku = '';
        var skuIds = [];
        if(location.href.match(/.*?:\/\/(.*)wong.pe\/cart(.*)/g) != null){
            for (var i=0;i<$('.product-item').length;i++)
            {
                try{
                    var skuId = $($('.product-item')[i]).data('id');
                    bdw_sku +='fq=skuId:' + skuId  + '&';
                    skuIds.push(skuId);
                }catch(e){}
            }
            bdw_sku += '&sc=' + bdwGetSucCookie();
        }
        else if(location.href.match(/.*?:\/\/(.*)wong.pe\/(.*)\/(p)/g) != null){
            bdw_sku = 'fq=skuId:' + skuJson_0.skus[0].sku +'&sc=' + bdwGetSucCookie();
        }
        
        console.log(bdw_sku);
        $.ajax({
            url: url,
            dataType: 'json',
            cache: false,
            async: true,
            timeout: 9000,
            data: bdw_sku,
            success: function (data) {
                try {
                    bdw_arbol_category ='';
                    if(location.href.match(/.*?:\/\/(.*)wong.pe\/cart(.*)/g) != null){
                        var productsFinded = [];
                        for (var j=0; j < skuIds.length; j++){
                            var filtered = data.filter(function(e) {
                              return e.items[0].itemId == skuIds[j];
                            });
                            productsFinded.push(filtered[0]);
                        }
                        
                        for (var i=0;i<productsFinded.length;i++)
                        {
                            bdw_arbol_category += productsFinded[i].categoriesIds[0];
                        }
                        var catNorepeat = '';
                        var arbdwarbolcategory=bdw_arbol_category.split('/');
                        for(var i=0;i<arbdwarbolcategory.length;i++)
                        {
                            if (catNorepeat.indexOf(arbdwarbolcategory[i])==-1 && arbdwarbolcategory[i]!='')
                            {
                                catNorepeat+= arbdwarbolcategory[i] + ",";
                            }                   
                        }
                        bdw_arbol_category = catNorepeat.replace(/,,/g,',');
                    }
                    else if(location.href.match(/.*?:\/\/(.*)wong.pe\/(.*)\/(p)/g) != null){
                        bdw_arbol_category = data[0].categoriesIds[0];
                    }
                    
                    console.log(bdw_arbol_category);
                }
                catch (e) { console.log(e)}
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) { console.log(thrownError);}
        });
    }catch(e){}
}

function BraindwRender(data, title, selector, eventName, sufix, itemCant, parentId, icon) {    
    var headerTitle = '';
    data=$.grep(data,function(n,i){return decodeURI(document.URL).indexOf(n.Link)===-1& n.Precio!=="0";});
    data = $.grep(data, function(element, index) {return element.Marca != "Wong"});
    
    if(selector != 'braindw_history'){
        var resto = data.length % itemCant;
        data.splice(data.length - resto, resto);
    }    
    if (data.length > 0) {        
        if(title != '')     
            headerTitle ='<div class="header clear-fix"><h2 class="title"><span class="%span-icon%"><a><img src="%iconUrlImage%" class=bw-icon></a></span><span class="text braindwtxt23">'+title+'</span></h2></div>'
        var templateGondolaProduct =
            '<section class="wrapper shop-list wfd_deparment" style="margin-bottom:40px;" id="'+parentId+'">' +
            '<div class="center">' + headerTitle + 
            '<div class="braindw_slider'+itemCant+'_gondolaproducts"><div class="braindw_slider'+itemCant+ ' '+selector+'" >';

        var itemproduct =
            '<li style="position: relative">' +
            '<div class="braindw_cucwm" style="display:%visibility_ahorro%">%CucardaOferta%</div>' +
            '<div class="bdw-cyberwong-cucarda" style="display:none;margin-top:-40px;width:50px"><img src="https://wongfood.vteximg.com.br/arquivos/Tag_CW_Wong.png" alt="cyberwong" class="bdw-cyberwong-img"></div>'+
            '<a href="%link%"  class="_braindwTriggerClick" bw-title="%Descripcion%" bw-section="'+eventName+'" bw-sku="%idcode%"><div class="braindw_hflag"><div class="flag %bnwTag0%"></div><div class="flag %bnwTag1%"></div><div class="flag %bnwTag2%"></div></div></a>' +
            '<a class="prateleira__image-link _braindwTriggerClick" bw-title="%Descripcion%" bw-section="'+eventName+'" bw-sku="%idcode%" href="%link%"><div class="prateleira__image"><img src="%urlImage%"></div></a>' +
            '<div class="product-item__flags">' +            
                '%cucas-flags-banderas%'+
            '</div>'+
            '<div class="product-item__flags bdw-flags" style="height: 56px;">' +
                '%cucas-flags%'+
            '</div>'+
            '<div class="prateleira  prateleira__content">' +
            '<a class="prateleira__name _braindwTriggerClick" bw-title="%Descripcion%" bw-section="'+eventName+'" bw-sku="%idcode%" href="%link%">%title%</a>' +
            '<a class="prateleira__marca _braindwTriggerClick" bw-title="%Descripcion%" bw-section="'+eventName+'" bw-sku="%idcode%" href="%link%">%brand%</a>' +
            '<a href="%link%" class="_braindwTriggerClick" bw-title="%Descripcion%" bw-section="'+eventName+'" bw-sku="%idcode%">' +
            '<braindwgdif class="braindwgdifct">' +
            '<div class="prateleira__list-price" style="visibility:%visibility_descuento%">Regular <span>%PrecioAnterior%</span></div> ' +
            '<div class="prateleira__best-price">Online <span>%price%</span></div>' +
            '</braindwgdif></a>' +
            '<div style="visibility:%visibility_preciokgltr%">(%PrecioKgLtr% x kg)</div>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div class="product-item__controls" style="visibility: %visibility_nostock%">' +
            '<div class="product-quantity">' +
            '<input id="cantProdBwnGond-%sufix%-%idcode%" type="text" class="product-quantity__input" value="%pesoproduct%" style="%styleAgregar%" onchange="BwdInputLimitCart(this, %saleNumber%)">' +
            '<input type="text" style="display:none;">' +
            '<input type="text" id="brandwProductGond-%sufix%-%idcode%" value="%pesoproduct%" style="display:none;">' +
            '<div class="braindw-product-quantity__controls" style="%styleAgregar2%">' +
            '<button id="addProductsBwnGond-IdCode" onclick="addProductsBwnGond(%idcode%, \'%sufix%\',%saleNumber%)" class="product-quantity__control--increase font-icn plus brandwMore"> </button>' +
            '<button id="clearProductsBwnGond-%sufix%-%idcode%" onclick="clearProductsBwnGond(%idcode%, \'%sufix%\')"  class="product-quantity__control--decrease font-icn minus brandwdecreasedisable"></button>' +
            '</div>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<button onclick="AddToMiniCartBraindGond(%AddTocart%, %idcode%,\'%sufix%\')" style="margin-left:5px;" class="product-item__add-to-cart product-add-to-cart btn add-to-cart braindw_addToCart _braindwTriggerClick" bw-title="%Descripcion%" bw-section="'+eventName+'" bw-sku="%idcode%" data-productid="%idcode%"><span class="font-icn check"></span>'+
            '<span class="product-add-to-cart__text product-add-to-cart__text--success">Agregado</span>'+
            '<span class="font-icn plus"></span><span class="font-icn shopping-cart"></span>'+
            '<span class="braindw-product-add-to-cart__text product-add-to-cart__text">Agregar</span>' +

            '</button>' +
            '<div class="product-item__cart-amount"><span class="font-icn check"></span><span class="value"></span></div>' +
            '</div>' +
            '</li>';

        var indice = 0;        
        var itemproductTopTen = '';
        var screencapture = screen.width;
        var cantitems = itemCant;
        if (screencapture <= 800 && screencapture >= 500) {
            cantitems = 3;
        } else if (screencapture < 500) {
            cantitems = 2;
        }

        var itemSinStock = '<div class="warning" style="margin-top:-5px;"><span class="font-icn attention" style="margin-top: 2px;"></span><span class="text" style="color:red;font-weight: bolder;margin-left: 2px;">Sin Stock</span></div>'
        if (icon != "") {
          templateGondolaProduct = templateGondolaProduct.replace("%iconUrlImage%", icon);
          templateGondolaProduct = templateGondolaProduct.replace("%span-icon%", "");
        }else{
          templateGondolaProduct = templateGondolaProduct.replace("%iconUrlImage%", "");          
        }

        $.each(data, function(i, item) {
            var customLink = item.Link; // + "?utm_source=" + _braindwUtmSource + "&utm_medium=" + _braindwUtmMedium + "&utm_campaign=" + _braindwUtmCampaign;
            var customItemGondolaProduct = itemproduct.replace("%brand%", item.Marca);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%srcImageCucardaExterna%", item.Image_CucardaUrlImageExterna);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%link%/g, customLink);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%urlImage%", item.UrlImagen);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%discount_description%", item.Articulo_Oferta);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%marca%", +item.Marca);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%linkCart%/g, item.addToCart);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%idcode%/g, item.IdArticulo);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%AddTocart%/g, "'" + item.addToCart + "'");
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%sufix%/g,sufix);            
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%saleNumber%/g, item.SaleNumber);
            if (item.PrecioKgLtr != null && item.PrecioKgLtr != '') {
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%price%", "S/" + item.PrecioKgLtr + " x kg");
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%Precio%/g, item.PrecioKgLtr + " x kg");
            } else {
                if (item.Precio != '0.00' && item.Precio != '0') {
                    customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%visibility_nostock%/g, 'visible');
                    customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%price%", "S/" + item.Precio);
                    customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%Precio%/g, item.Precio);
                } else {
                    customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%visibility_nostock%/g, 'hidden');
                    customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace('<div class="prateleira__best-price">Online <span>%price%</span></div>', itemSinStock);
                }
            }
            if (item.CucardaOferta != null && item.CucardaOferta != '') {
                var porProduct = item.CucardaOferta;
                porProduct = porProduct.replace('%', '');
                if (porProduct.indexOf('.')) {
                    porProduct = porProduct.split('.')[0]
                }
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%CucardaOferta%", "-" + porProduct + "%");
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace('Ahorro', '');
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%visibility_ahorro%/g, 'block');
            } else {
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%CucardaOferta%", '');
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%visibility_ahorro%/g, 'none');
            }
            if (item.PrecioKgLtr != null && item.PrecioKgLtr != '') {
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%PrecioKgLtr%/g, item.PrecioKgLtr);
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%visibility_preciokgltr%/g, "hidden");
            } else {
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%PrecioKgLtr%/g, '');
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%visibility_preciokgltr%/g, "hidden");
            }

            var cucas = '';
            var cucasBanderas = '';
            if (item.Descuento_Descripcion != null && item.Descuento_Descripcion != '') {
                var arTags = item.Descuento_Descripcion.split('|');                
                for (var bwnIndex = 0; bwnIndex < arTags.length; bwnIndex++) {
                    customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%bnwTag" + bwnIndex + "%", arTags[bwnIndex]);
                    var cucardaReplace = arTags[bwnIndex].replace(/ /g, '-').toLowerCase();

                    if (cucardaReplace.indexOf('bandera') > -1|| cucardaReplace.indexOf('48horas') > -1) {
                        cucasBanderas += '<p class="flag '+cucardaReplace+'"></p>';
                    }
                    if (cucardaReplace.indexOf('octogonal') > -1){
                        cucas += '<p class="flag '+cucardaReplace+'"></p>';
                    }
                }
            }
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace('%cucas-flags%', cucas);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace('%cucas-flags-banderas%', cucasBanderas);

            if (item.PrecioAnterior != '') {
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%PrecioAnterior%", 'S/' + item.PrecioAnterior);
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%visibility_descuento%", 'visible');
            } else
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%visibility_descuento%", 'hidden');

            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%PrecioAnterior%", item.PrecioAnterior);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace("%title%", item.Descripcion);
            customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%Descripcion%/g, item.Descripcion);

            if (item.UnidadPrecio != null && item.UnidadPrecio != '1' && item.UnidadPrecio != '1.00') {
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace('%unidadventa%', 'Unidad(1)= ' + item.UnidadPrecio + 'kg');
            } else {
                if (item.UnidadPrecio == null || item.UnidadPrecio == 'null') item.UnidadPrecio = 1;
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%pesoproduct%/g, item.UnidadPrecio);
                customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace('%unidadventa%', '');
            }

            switch (item.PrecioKgLtrUnidad) {
                case "un":                    
                    customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%pesoproduct%/g, item.UnidadPrecio);
                    break;
                case "kg":                    
                    customItemGondolaProduct = customItemGondolaProduct.replace(/%pesoproduct%/g, item.UnidadPrecio + " kg");
                    break;
            }

            itemproductTopTen += customItemGondolaProduct;
            indice++;
            if (indice == cantitems) {                
                templateGondolaProduct = templateGondolaProduct + '<div><ul>' + itemproductTopTen + '</ul></div>';
                indice = 0;        
                itemproductTopTen = '';                        
            }
        });

        if (indice > 0 && indice != cantitems) {
            templateGondolaProduct = templateGondolaProduct + '<div><ul>' + itemproductTopTen + '</ul></div>';
        }
        templateGondolaProduct = templateGondolaProduct + '</div></div></div></div></section>';

        return templateGondolaProduct;
    }
    return "";
}
